<span style=""><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Family_of_the_United_States" title="First Family of the United States">U.S. First Family</a> (2011): <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, Sasha Obama, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michelle_Obama" title="Michelle Obama">Michelle Obama</a>, and Malia Obama.</span></td>
</tr>

<p>The <b>family of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a></b>, the 44th <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> of America, is made up of people of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African_American" title="African American">African American</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_American" title="English American">English</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenyan</a> (<a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luo_(Kenya_and_Tanzania)" title="Luo (Kenya and Tanzania)" class="mw-redirect">Luo</a>), and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_people" title="Irish people">Irish</a> heritage,<sup id="cite_ref-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-0"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup> who are known through Obama's writings and other reports.<sup id="cite_ref-Reitwiesner_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reitwiesner-2"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup> His immediate family is the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Family_of_the_United_States" title="First Family of the United States">First Family of the United States</a>. The Obamas are the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_African_American_firsts" title="List of African American firsts" class="mw-redirect">first</a> First Family of African descent.</p>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Immediate_family">Immediate family</span></h2>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Michelle_Obama"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michelle_Obama" title="Michelle Obama">Michelle Obama</a></dt>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Michelle Obama, née Robinson, the wife of Barack Obama, was born on January&#160;17, 1964 in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicago,_Illinois" title="Chicago, Illinois" class="mw-redirect">Chicago, Illinois</a>. She is a lawyer and was a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago_Hospitals" title="University of Chicago Hospitals" class="mw-redirect">University of Chicago Hospital</a> vice-president. She is the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Lady_of_the_United_States" title="First Lady of the United States">First Lady of the United States</a>.</dd>
</dl>
<p><span id="Malia_Obama"></span><span id="Sasha_Obama"></span><span id="Malia_and_Sasha_Obama"></span><span id="Sasha_and_Malia_Obama"></span></p>
<dl>
<dt>Malia Obama and Sasha Obama</dt>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Barack and Michelle Obama have two daughters: Malia Ann <span class="nowrap"><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English">/</a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="'m' in 'my'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">m</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="schwa 'a' in 'about'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ə</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="primary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˈ</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="'l' in 'lie'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">l</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="long 'e' in 'bead'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">iː</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="schwa 'a' in 'about'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ə</span></a></span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English">/</a></span></span>, born on July&#160;4, 1998,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> and Natasha (known as Sasha <span class="nowrap"><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English">/</a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="primary stress follows" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ˈ</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="'s' in 'sigh'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">s</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="'a' in 'father'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ɑː</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="'sh' in 'shy'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ʃ</span></a></span><span class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English#Key" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English"><span title="schwa 'a' in 'about'" style="border-bottom:1px dotted">ə</span></a></span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:IPA_for_English" title="Wikipedia:IPA for English">/</a></span></span>), born on June&#160;10, 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup> They were both delivered by their parents' friend Dr. Anita Blanchard at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago_Medical_Center" title="University of Chicago Medical Center">University of Chicago Medical Center</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup> Sasha is the youngest child to reside in the White House since <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_F._Kennedy,_Jr." title="John F. Kennedy, Jr.">John&#160;F. Kennedy,&#160;Jr.</a> arrived as an infant in 1961.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Before his inauguration, President Obama published an open letter to his daughters in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parade_magazine" title="Parade magazine" class="mw-redirect"><i>Parade</i></a> magazine, describing what he wants for them and every child in America: "to grow up in a world with no limits on your dreams and no achievements beyond your reach, and to grow into compassionate, committed women who will help build that world."<sup id="cite_ref-daughters1_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-daughters1-10"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>While living in Chicago, the Obamas kept busy schedules, as the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Associated_Press" title="Associated Press">Associated Press</a> reports: "soccer, dance and drama for Malia, gymnastics and tap for Sasha, piano and tennis for both."<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup> In July 2008, the family gave an interview to the television series <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Access_Hollywood" title="Access Hollywood">Access Hollywood</a></i>. Obama later said they regretted allowing the children to be included.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd><span class="nowrap">Malia and Sasha</span> attend the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Independent_school" title="Independent school">private</a> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sidwell_Friends_School" title="Sidwell Friends School">Sidwell Friends School</a> in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Washington,_DC" title="Washington, DC" class="mw-redirect">Washington,&#160;DC</a>, the same school as attended by <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chelsea_Clinton" title="Chelsea Clinton">Chelsea Clinton</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tricia_Nixon_Cox" title="Tricia Nixon Cox">Tricia Nixon Cox</a>, and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Archibald_Roosevelt" title="Archibald Roosevelt">Archibald Roosevelt</a>, and currently the grandchildren of Vice President <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joe_Biden" title="Joe Biden">Joe Biden</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> The Obama girls began classes there on January&#160;5, 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-start-sidwell09_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-start-sidwell09-15"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup> While in Chicago, both attended the private <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago_Laboratory_School" title="University of Chicago Laboratory School" class="mw-redirect">University of Chicago Laboratory School</a>.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>In his victory speech on the night of his election, President Obama repeated his promise to Sasha and Malia to get a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_presidential_pets" title="List of presidential pets" class="mw-redirect">puppy</a> to take with them to the White House.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup> The selection was slow because Malia is <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Allergies" title="Allergies" class="mw-redirect">allergic</a> to animal <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dander" title="Dander">dander</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup> the president subsequently said that the choice had been narrowed down to either a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Labradoodle" title="Labradoodle">labradoodle</a> or <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_Water_Dog" title="Portuguese Water Dog">Portuguese Water Dog</a>, and they hoped to find a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Animal_shelter" title="Animal shelter">shelter</a> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rescue_dog" title="Rescue dog">animal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup> On April 12, 2009, it was reported that the Obamas had adopted a six-month-old Portuguese Water Dog given to them as a gift from Senator <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ted_Kennedy" title="Ted Kennedy">Ted Kennedy</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-splash_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-splash-19"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup> the dog was named <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bo_(dog)" title="Bo (dog)">Bo</a> by Malia and Sasha.<sup id="cite_ref-splash_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-splash-19"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marian_Shields_Robinson" title="Marian Shields Robinson" class="mw-redirect">Marian Robinson</a></dt>
<dd>Marian Robinson, Barack Obama's mother-in-law, is currently residing in the White House. She is part of the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Family_of_Barack_Obama#Michelle_Robinson_Obama.27s_extended_family" title="Family of Barack Obama">Robinson family (see below)</a>.</dd>
</dl>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Maternal_relations">Maternal relations</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Ann_Dunham_with_father_and_children_(enhanced).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e5/Ann_Dunham_with_father_and_children_%28enhanced%29.jpg/220px-Ann_Dunham_with_father_and_children_%28enhanced%29.jpg" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Ann_Dunham_with_father_and_children_(enhanced).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://bits.wikimedia.org/skins-1.19/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt=""/></a></div>
<i>Right-to-left:</i> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_Soetoro-Ng" title="Maya Soetoro-Ng">Maya Soetoro</a> with their mother <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ann_Dunham" title="Ann Dunham">Ann Dunham</a> and grandfather <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madelyn_and_Stanley_Dunham" title="Madelyn and Stanley Dunham" class="mw-redirect">Stanley Dunham</a> in Hawaii (early 1970s)</div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="metadata mbox-small plainlinks" style="border:1px solid #aaa; background-color:#f9f9f9;">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikinews-logo.svg/40px-Wikinews-logo.svg.png" width="40" height="23"/></td>
<td class="mbox-text" style="">Wikinews has related news:
<ul>
<li><i><b><a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikinews.org/wiki/Barack_Obama_elected_44th_President_of_the_United_States">Barack Obama elected 44th President of the United States</a></b></i></li>
<li><i><b><a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikinews.org/wiki/Grandmother_of_Barack_Obama_dies_at_86">Grandmother of Barack Obama dies at 86</a></b></i></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>Barack Obama was raised by his mother <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanley_Ann_Dunham" title="Stanley Ann Dunham" class="mw-redirect">Stanley Ann Dunham</a> and grandparents <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madelyn_Dunham" title="Madelyn Dunham">Madelyn</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanley_Armour_Dunham" title="Stanley Armour Dunham">Stanley Armour Dunham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-freespirit_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-freespirit-20"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup> He has often referred to his family during his candidacy and term as President.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Ann_Dunham"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ann_Dunham" title="Ann Dunham">Ann Dunham</a></dt>
<dd>Mother of Barack Obama born in 1942, died in 1995. Born Stanley Ann Dunham, she was an American <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthropologist" title="Anthropologist" class="mw-redirect">anthropologist</a> who specialized in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Economic_anthropology" title="Economic anthropology">economic anthropology</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rural_development" title="Rural development">rural development</a>. She earned her <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ph.D" title="Ph.D" class="mw-redirect">Ph.D</a> from the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Hawaii" title="University of Hawaii">University of Hawaii</a> and worked with the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Agency_for_International_Development" title="United States Agency for International Development">United States Agency for International Development</a>, the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ford_Foundation" title="Ford Foundation">Ford Foundation</a>, and Women's World Banking, championing <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microcredit" title="Microcredit">microcredit</a> for the world’s poor.<sup id="cite_ref-freespirit_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-freespirit-20"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-duke_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-duke-25"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup> The Ann Dunham Soetoro Endowment in the Anthropology Department at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Hawai%CA%BBi_at_M%C4%81noa" title="University of Hawaiʻi at Mānoa">University of Hawaiʻi at Mānoa</a> and the Ann Dunham Soetoro Graduate Fellowships at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East%E2%80%93West_Center" title="East–West Center">East–West Center</a> (EWC) in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honolulu,_Hawaii" title="Honolulu, Hawaii" class="mw-redirect">Honolulu, Hawaii</a> are named in her honor.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Ann_Dunham_Soetoro_Endowed_Fund_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Ann_Dunham_Soetoro_Endowed_Fund-26"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup> Obama refers to his mother as the dominant figure in his formative years. "The values she taught me continue to be my touchstone when it comes to how I go about the world of politics." <sup id="cite_ref-notjustagirl_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-notjustagirl-27"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Stanley_Armour_Dunham"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanley_Armour_Dunham" title="Stanley Armour Dunham">Stanley Armour Dunham</a></dt>
<dd>Stanley Dunham is the grandfather of Barack Obama. He was born in 1918 and served as a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sergeant" title="Sergeant">sergeant</a> in the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Army" title="U.S. Army" class="mw-redirect">U.S. Army</a> during <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, enlisting just after the attacks on <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pearl_Harbor" title="Pearl Harbor">Pearl Harbor</a>. Stanley and his wife <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madelyn_Dunham" title="Madelyn Dunham">Madelyn</a> raised Obama in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honolulu,_Hawaii" title="Honolulu, Hawaii" class="mw-redirect">Honolulu, Hawaii</a>. In addition to Obama, Stanley is related to six US presidents: <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Madison" title="James Madison">James Madison</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Truman" title="Harry Truman" class="mw-redirect">Harry Truman</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lyndon_Johnson" title="Lyndon Johnson" class="mw-redirect">Lyndon Johnson</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jimmy_Carter" title="Jimmy Carter">Jimmy Carter</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">George H. W. Bush</a>, and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup> He died in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honolulu,_Hawaii" title="Honolulu, Hawaii" class="mw-redirect">Honolulu, Hawaii</a>, in 1992, and is buried at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Punchbowl_National_Cemetery" title="Punchbowl National Cemetery" class="mw-redirect">Punchbowl National Cemetery</a>.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Ralph_Dunham"></span>Ralph Dunham</dt>
<dd>Great-uncle of Barack Obama, older brother of Stanley Dunham, born 1916. He served in the U.S. Army as an assignment and personnel officer during World War II, landing at Normandy's Omaha Easy Red Beach on D-Day plus four, working his way through France, Italy and Germany.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span>[</span>31<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span>[</span>32<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Madelyn_Lee_Payne_Dunham"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madelyn_Lee_Payne_Dunham" title="Madelyn Lee Payne Dunham" class="mw-redirect">Madelyn Lee Payne Dunham</a></dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's maternal grandmother was born in 1922 and died on November 2, 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup> She was a bank vice president in Hawaii. Obama said that when he was a child, his grandmother "read me the opening lines of the Declaration of Independence and told me about the men and women who marched for equality because they believed those words put to paper two centuries ago should mean something."<sup id="cite_ref-daughters1_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-daughters1-10"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup> According to Barack Obama's <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dreams_from_My_Father" title="Dreams from My Father">Dreams from My Father</a>,</i><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup> his great-grandmother Leona McCurry was part <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">Native American</a>, which Obama believed Leona held as a "source of considerable shame" and "blanched whenever someone mentioned the subject and hoped to carry the secret to her grave"; whereas McCurry's daughter (Obama's maternal grandmother) "would turn her head in profile to show off her beaked nose, which along with a pair of jet-black eyes, was offered as proof of Cherokee blood."<sup id="cite_ref-gma_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gma-34"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup> To date, no concrete evidence has surfaced of Cherokee heritage. Obama's maternal heritage consists mostly of English ancestry, with much smaller amounts of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_American" title="German American">German</a>, Irish, Scottish, Welsh, Swiss, and French ancestry.<sup id="cite_ref-Reitwiesner_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reitwiesner-2"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Jonathan_Singletary_Dunham"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Singletary_Dunham" title="Jonathan Singletary Dunham">Jonathan Singletary Dunham</a></dt>
<dd>Born in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massachusetts_Bay_Colony" title="Massachusetts Bay Colony">Massachusetts Bay Colony</a> in 1640, Barack Obama's 8-greats-grandfather was his earliest ancestor born in North America.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Charles_T._Payne"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_T._Payne" title="Charles T. Payne">Charles Thomas Payne</a></dt>
<dd>Great-uncle of Barack Obama, younger brother of Madelyn Dunham, born 1925. Served during World War II in the U.S. Army <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/89th_Division_(United_States)" title="89th Division (United States)" class="mw-redirect">89th Infantry Division</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup> Obama has often described Payne's role in liberating <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ohrdruf_forced_labor_camp" title="Ohrdruf forced labor camp" class="mw-redirect">Ohrdruf forced labor camp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-bostonobamauncle_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bostonobamauncle-36"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup> There was brief media attention when Obama mistakenly identified the camp as <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Auschwitz_concentration_camp" title="Auschwitz concentration camp">Auschwitz</a> during the campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2009, Payne spoke about this experiences:
<blockquote>
<p>Ohrdruf was in that string of towns going across, south of Gotha and Erfurt. Our division was the first one in there. When we arrived there were no German soldiers anywhere around that I knew about. There was no fighting against the Germans, no camp guards. The whole area was overrun by people from the camp dressed in the most pitiful rags, and most of them were in a bad state of starvation.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</blockquote>
Payne appeared in the visitor's gallery at the Democratic National Convention in Denver, Colorado, when his great-nephew was nominated for President.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup> He was the assistant director of the University of Chicago's Library.<sup id="cite_ref-bostonobamauncle_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bostonobamauncle-36"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Maya_Soetoro-Ng"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_Soetoro-Ng" title="Maya Soetoro-Ng">Maya Soetoro-Ng</a></dt>
<dd>Half-sister of Barack Obama, born August 15, 1970, in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup> She has another half-brother, Yusuf, and a half-sister, Aya, from her father's second marriage. She is married to Konrad Ng, with whom she has two daughters, Suhaila and Savita. Maya Soetoro-Ng is a teacher in Hawaii.<sup id="cite_ref-SisterWash_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SisterWash-41"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Konrad_Ng"></span>Konrad Ng</dt>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Brother-in-law of Barack Obama, born 1974. He is of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malaysian_Chinese" title="Malaysian Chinese">Malaysian Chinese</a> descent,<sup id="cite_ref-thespec_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thespec-42"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup> and his parents are from <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kudat" title="Kudat">Kudat</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sandakan" title="Sandakan">Sandakan</a>, two small towns in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sabah,_Malaysia" title="Sabah, Malaysia" class="mw-redirect">Sabah, Malaysia</a>. Ng and his younger brother, Perry, were born and raised in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burlington,_Ontario" title="Burlington, Ontario">Burlington</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ontario" title="Ontario">Ontario</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup> Perry Ng works for the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Ottawa" title="University of Ottawa">University of Ottawa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-thespec_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thespec-42"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup> He married Maya Soetoro-Ng at the end of 2003 in Hawaii.<sup id="cite_ref-handle_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-handle-44"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup> They have two daughters, Suhaila<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup> and Savita.<sup id="cite_ref-SisterWash_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SisterWash-41"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup> Konrad Ng currently is a US citizen.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup> He is an assistant professor at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Hawaii" title="University of Hawaii">University of Hawaii</a>'s Academy of Creative Media.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup> He studied philosophy at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/McGill_University" title="McGill University">McGill University</a> and cultural studies at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Victoria" title="University of Victoria">University of Victoria</a> before he got his PhD from University of Hawaii at Manoa.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Lolo_Soetoro"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lolo_Soetoro" title="Lolo Soetoro">Lolo Soetoro</a></dt>
<dd>The second husband of Ann Dunham and stepfather to Barack Obama, born in Indonesia 1936, died 1987. He is the father of Maya Soetoro-Ng. After his divorce from Dunham, Soetoro married Erna Kustina. She bore him two children, Yusuf Aji Soetoro (b. 1981) and Rahayu Nurmaida Soetoro (b. 1984).<sup id="cite_ref-JawaPos2_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JawaPos2-52"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Robert_Wolfley"></span>Robert Wolfley</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's great-great-great-grandfather. He served as a private in Company A, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/145th_Ohio_Infantry" title="145th Ohio Infantry">145th Ohio Infantry</a> during the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Civil_War" title="American Civil War">American Civil War</a>. He is buried in the Olathe Memorial Cemetery in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Olathe,_Kansas" title="Olathe, Kansas">Olathe, Kansas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Paternal_relations">Paternal relations</span></h2>
<p>The Obamas are members of the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luo_(Kenya_and_Tanzania)" title="Luo (Kenya and Tanzania)" class="mw-redirect">Luo</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>'s third-largest ethnic group, which is part of a larger family of ethnic groups, collectively also known as <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luo_(family_of_ethnic_groups)" title="Luo (family of ethnic groups)" class="mw-redirect">Luo</a>. Linguistically, the Luo language belongs to the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eastern_Sudanic_languages" title="Eastern Sudanic languages">Eastern Sudanic</a> branch of the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nilo-Saharan_languages" title="Nilo-Saharan languages">Nilo-Saharan</a> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phylum_(linguistics)" title="Phylum (linguistics)" class="mw-redirect">phylum</a>. The Obama family is largely concentrated in the western province of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyanza_Province" title="Nyanza Province">Nyanza</a>.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Barack_Obama%27s_Kenyan_relatives.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a3/Barack_Obama%27s_Kenyan_relatives.jpg/250px-Barack_Obama%27s_Kenyan_relatives.jpg" width="250" height="176" class="thumbimage"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Barack_Obama%27s_Kenyan_relatives.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://bits.wikimedia.org/skins-1.19/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt=""/></a></div>
<b>Front row (left to right):</b> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Auma_Obama" title="Auma Obama" class="mw-redirect">Auma Obama</a> (Barack's half-sister), <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kezia_Obama" title="Kezia Obama" class="mw-redirect">Kezia Obama</a> (Barack's stepmother), <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Onyango_Obama" title="Sarah Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Sarah Hussein Onyango Obama</a> (third wife of Barack's paternal grandfather), <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zeituni_Onyango" title="Zeituni Onyango">Zeituni Onyango</a> (Barack's aunt)<br/>
<b>Back row (left to right):</b> Sayid Obama (Barack's uncle), <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malik_Obama" title="Malik Obama" class="mw-redirect">Abongo [Roy] Obama</a> (Barack's half-brother), unidentified woman, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bernard_Obama" title="Bernard Obama" class="mw-redirect">Bernard Obama</a> (Barack's half-brother), <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abo_Obama" title="Abo Obama" class="mw-redirect">Abo Obama</a> (Barack's half-brother).</div>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Barack_Obama.2C_Sr."></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barack_Obama,_Sr." title="Barack Obama, Sr.">Barack Obama, Sr.</a></dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's father (1936–1982). Government economist in Kenya. In addition to President Obama, Barack Obama Sr. fathered one daughter and at least four sons.<sup id="cite_ref-genealogy_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-genealogy-54"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Sarah_Obama_.28aunt_of_Barack_Obama.29"></span>Sarah Obama (aunt of Barack Obama)</dt>
<dd>Aunt of U.S. President Barack Obama and elder sister of his father, born 1933 to Hussein Onyango and Habiba Akumu Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams_from_my_Father.2C_p._408_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams_from_my_Father.2C_p._408-55"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup> (She should not be confused with her stepmother <a href="#Sarah_Onyango_Obama">Sarah Onyango Obama</a>, also often called just Sarah Obama, the third wife of Onyango.)</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Hawa_Auma_Hussein_.28aunt_of_Barack_Obama.29"></span>Hawa Auma Hussein (aunt of Barack Obama)</dt>
<dd>Aunt of U.S. President Barack Obama and younger sister of his father, born to Hussein Onyango and Habiba Akumu Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams_from_my_Father.2C_p._408_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams_from_my_Father.2C_p._408-55"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup> She is the sole surviving full sibling of Barack Obama, Sr.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span>[</span>57<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Hussein_Onyango_Obama"></span>Hussein Onyango Obama</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's paternal grandfather (c. 1895–1979).<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span>[</span>58<span>]</span></a></sup> (One source gives 1870–1975 as his dates of birth and death, possibly based on his tombstone in his home village.,<sup id="cite_ref-allafrica1_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-allafrica1-58"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup> In 1988 Barack Obama found a British document based on a 1928 ordinance recording his grandfather as 35 years old. The date of the document must have been around 1930, which means that his grandfather had indeed been born around 1895.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span>[</span>60<span>]</span></a></sup>) Onyango was the fifth son of his mother, Nyaoke, who was the first of the five wives of his father, Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60"><span>[</span>61<span>]</span></a></sup> Barack Obama relates how his step-grandmother Granny Sarah (<a href="#Sarah_Onyango_Obama">Sarah Onyango Obama</a>) describes his grandfather: "Even from the time that he was a boy, your grandfather Onyango was strange. It is said of him that he had ants up his anus, because he could not sit still."<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams.2C_p._397_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams.2C_p._397-61"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup> As a young man, he learned to speak, read and write in English.<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams.2C_p._400_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams.2C_p._400-62"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Onyango worked as a mission cook and as a local <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herbalist" title="Herbalist">herbalist</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams.2C_p._397_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams.2C_p._397-61"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup> He joined the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King%27s_African_Rifles" title="King's African Rifles">King's African Rifles</a><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup> during <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>In 1949, Onyango spent at least 6 months in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kamiti_Maximum_Security_Prison" title="Kamiti Maximum Security Prison">Kamiti Prison</a>. He was probably tried in a magistrates’ court on charges of political sedition or membership of a banned organisation, but the records do not survive, because all such documentation was routinely destroyed in British colonies after six years. He was tortured to extract information about the growing insurgency.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup> In his memoir, President Obama described his grandfather's shocking physical state: "When he returned to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siaya_District" title="Siaya District">Alego</a> he was very thin and dirty. He had difficulty walking, and his head was full of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Head_lice" title="Head lice" class="mw-redirect">lice</a>." For some time, he was too traumatized to speak about his experiences. His wife told his grandson: "From that day on, I saw that he was now an old man."<sup id="cite_ref-Dreams.2C_p._400_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dreams.2C_p._400-62"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup> Onyango was permanently scarred, remaining in pain and requiring assistance moving until his death. Although previously working very closely with British colonists, his torture left Onyango bitterly anti-British. During a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sky_News" title="Sky News">Sky News</a> interview in 2009, Barack Obama was asked if this negatively affected his view of the British personally and he replied that it did not. "I love the Brits and I think I have shown that affection every time I have visited there. The notion that I would somehow judge countries based on what happened 100 years ago would not make much sense."<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Onyango is sometimes referred to as Mzee Hussein Onyango Obama. The word <i>mzee</i> is a Kenyan <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honorific" title="Honorific">honorific</a> meaning "old man" or "elder."</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>According to his third wife, Sarah, he originally converted to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman_Catholic" title="Roman Catholic" class="mw-redirect">Catholicism</a>, but took the name <i>Hussein</i> when he later converted to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islam</a>; she said he passed the name, not the religion, on to his children.<sup id="cite_ref-AP-obama-kin_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AP-obama-kin-66"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup> Luos are given names related to the circumstances of their birth, and <i>Onyango</i> means born in the early morning.<sup id="cite_ref-Luo_surnames_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luo_surnames-67"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Obama%27s_Grandmother.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Obama%27s_Grandmother.jpg/100px-Obama%27s_Grandmother.jpg" width="100" height="254" class="thumbimage"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Obama%27s_Grandmother.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://bits.wikimedia.org/skins-1.19/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt=""/></a></div>
Habiba Akumu Obama</div>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Habiba_Akumu_Obama"></span>Habiba Akumu Obama</dt>
<dd>Also known as Akumu Nyanjoga (c. 1918-2006).<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>70<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-eastandard.net_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eastandard.net-71"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup> Barack Obama's paternal grandmother, and the second wife of Hussein Onyango Obama. She gave Onyango three children: daughters Sarah and Auma, and son Barack (Barack Obama's father).<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72"><span>[</span>73<span>]</span></a></sup> Her father was named Njango and she was born and raised in the Western Kenyan village of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karachuonyo_Constituency" title="Karachuonyo Constituency">Karabondi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-eastandard.net_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eastandard.net-71"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span>[</span>74<span>]</span></a></sup> In his memoir <i>Dreams from My Father,</i> her grandson wrote that she was miserable in her marriage and abandoned her husband and children and subsequently married again and moved to present-day Tanzania. Luos are given names related to the circumstances of their birth and <i>Akumu</i> means mysterious birth, a conception after a birth, but before resumption of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Menses" title="Menses" class="mw-redirect">menses</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Luo_surnames_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luo_surnames-67"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup> She took the name Habiba upon her conversion to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islam</a>. A photograph of her holding her son, Barack Sr, on her lap is on the cover of her grandson's memoir. (See image at right margin.)<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74"><span>[</span>75<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Sarah_Onyango_Obama"></span>Sarah Onyango Obama</dt>
<dd>Third wife of Obama's paternal grandfather, born 1922.<sup id="cite_ref-allafrica1_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-allafrica1-58"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup> She is known for short as Sarah Obama and is sometimes referred to as Sarah Ogwel, Sarah Hussein Obama or Sarah Anyango Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-Time_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-75"><span>[</span>76<span>]</span></a></sup> She lives in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyang%E2%80%99oma_Kogelo" title="Nyang’oma Kogelo">Nyang’oma Kogelo</a> village, 30 miles west of western <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>'s main town, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kisumu" title="Kisumu">Kisumu</a>, on the edge of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lake_Victoria" title="Lake Victoria">Lake Victoria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76"><span>[</span>77<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-chicsuntimes_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chicsuntimes-77"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup> (She should not be confused with her stepdaughter of the same name, <a href="#Sarah_Obama_.28aunt_of_Barack_Obama.29">Sarah Obama</a>, a daughter of Onyango's second wife, Akumu.)<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78"><span>[</span>79<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Although she is not a blood relation, Barack Obama calls her "Granny Sarah".<sup id="cite_ref-Time_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-75"><span>[</span>76<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CNN_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CNN-79"><span>[</span>80<span>]</span></a></sup> Sarah, who speaks <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dholuo_language" title="Dholuo language" class="mw-redirect">Luo</a> and only a few words of English, communicates with President Obama through an interpreter.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>On July 4, 2008, she attended the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Independence_Day_(United_States)" title="Independence Day (United States)">United States Independence Day</a> celebrations in Nairobi, hosted by Michael Ranneberger, the US ambassador in Kenya.<sup id="cite_ref-granny_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-granny-80"><span>[</span>81<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>During the campaign she protested attempts to portray Obama as a foreigner to the United States or a Muslim, saying that while Obama's grandfather had been a Muslim, "In the world of today, children have different religions from their parents."<sup id="cite_ref-AP-obama-kin_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AP-obama-kin-66"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup> Sarah Obama herself is "a strong believer of the Islamic faith,” in her words.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Kezia_Obama"></span>Kezia Obama</dt>
<dd>(Also known as Kezia Aoko<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup> and as "Grace"<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup>). Born c. 1940, she is Barack Obama Sr.'s first wife, whom he married in Kenya before studying abroad in the United States. She currently lives in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bracknell" title="Bracknell">Bracknell</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berkshire" title="Berkshire">Berkshire</a>, England.<sup id="cite_ref-dailymail.co.uk_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dailymail.co.uk-85"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbc-new-kezia-obama_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-new-kezia-obama-86"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup> On March 22, 2009, Kezia made a guest appearance on the British television show <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chris_Moyles%27_Quiz_Night" title="Chris Moyles' Quiz Night">Chris Moyles' Quiz Night</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup> Her sister, Jane, is the 'Auntie Jane' mentioned at the very start of <i>Dreams from My Father</i> when she telephoned Obama to inform him that his father had been killed in a car accident.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Malik_Obama"></span>Malik Obama</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's half-brother, also known as Abongo or Roy, born c. March 1958,<sup id="cite_ref-dailymail.co.uk_85-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dailymail.co.uk-85"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup> son of Barack Obama, Sr. with his first wife, Kezia.<sup id="cite_ref-factcheck_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-factcheck-89"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup> Malik Obama was born and raised in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> He earned a degree in accounting from the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Nairobi" title="University of Nairobi">University of Nairobi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup> He met his half-brother for the first time in 1985<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> when Barack flew from Chicago to Washington, D.C., to visit him.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup> Malik and his half-brother Barack were <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Best_man" title="Best man" class="mw-redirect">best men</a> at each other's weddings.<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> Barack Obama brought his wife Michelle to Kenya three years later, and they met with Malik again while Barack was introducing Michelle to many other new relatives.<sup id="cite_ref-sleepy_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sleepy-93"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>Although much of the Obama family has dispersed throughout Kenya and overseas, most, including Malik Obama, still considered their rural village on the shores of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lake_Victoria" title="Lake Victoria">Lake Victoria</a> to be their true home, and feel that those who have left the village have become culturally "lost".<sup id="cite_ref-Ochieng_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ochieng-94"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup> A frequent visitor to the United States,<sup id="cite_ref-sleepy_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sleepy-93"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup> and consultant in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> for several months per year,<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> he nevertheless settled in the Obamas' ancestral home, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyang%E2%80%99oma_Kogelo" title="Nyang’oma Kogelo">Nyang’oma Kogelo</a>, a village of several hundred people that he prefers to the city for its slow pace.<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> He runs a small electronics shop a half hour drive outside of town.<sup id="cite_ref-slowlane_90-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-slowlane-90"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dd>During his brother's presidential campaign, Malik Obama was a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spokesman" title="Spokesman" class="mw-redirect">spokesman</a> for the extended Obama family in Kenya, dealing with safety and privacy concerns arising from increased attention from the press.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Auma_Obama"></span>Auma Obama</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's half-sister, born c. 1960.<sup id="cite_ref-Auma_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Auma-96"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup> As of July 2008, development worker in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-spiegeljul08_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spiegeljul08-97"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup> She studied German at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Heidelberg" title="University of Heidelberg" class="mw-redirect">University of Heidelberg</a> from 1981 to 1987. After her graduation in Heidelberg she went on for graduate studies at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Bayreuth" title="University of Bayreuth">University of Bayreuth</a>, which awarded her a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PhD" title="PhD" class="mw-redirect">PhD</a> in 1996. Her <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dissertation" title="Dissertation" class="mw-redirect">dissertation</a> was about the conception of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Labour_(economics)" title="Labour (economics)" class="mw-redirect">labor</a> in Germany and its literary reflections.<sup id="cite_ref-spiegeljul08_97-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spiegeljul08-97"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup> Auma Obama has lived in London, and in 1996 married an <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_people" title="English people">Englishman</a>, Ian Manners, although they have since divorced.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98"><span>[</span>99<span>]</span></a></sup> They have a daughter named Akinyi (b. 1997).<sup id="cite_ref-spiegeljul08_97-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spiegeljul08-97"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99"><span>[</span>100<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2011 Auma Obama was interviewed for <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turk_Pipkin" title="Turk Pipkin">Turk Pipkin</a>'s documentary <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Building_Hope" title="Building Hope">Building Hope</a>.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Abo_Obama"></span>Abo Obama</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's alleged half-brother also known as Samson Obama,<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup> born 1968. In <i>Dreams from My Father</i>, it is stated that the Obama family doubt Abo and Bernard are the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paternity_(biology_and_medicine)" title="Paternity (biology and medicine)" class="mw-redirect">biological sons</a> of Barack Obama, Sr. Abo is a mobile phone shop manager in Kenya.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101"><span>[</span>102<span>]</span></a></sup> He was barred from entering the United Kingdom after receiving a police caution for a public order offence; he was also accused of but not prosecuted for sexual assault. At the time he had been living illegally in the UK.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102"><span>[</span>103<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Bernard_Obama"></span>Bernard Obama</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's alleged half-brother, born 1970. <i>Dreams from My Father</i> states that the Obama family doubt Abo and Bernard are the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paternity_(biology_and_medicine)" title="Paternity (biology and medicine)" class="mw-redirect">biological sons</a> of Barack Obama, Sr. He had been an auto parts supplier in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nairobi,_Kenya" title="Nairobi, Kenya" class="mw-redirect">Nairobi, Kenya</a>, and has one child. Bernard converted to Islam as an adult and has said: "I’m a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslim</a>, I don’t deny it. My father was raised a Muslim. But it’s not an issue. I don’t know what all the hullabaloo is about."<sup id="cite_ref-oliver_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oliver-104"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup> He currently resides in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bracknell" title="Bracknell">Bracknell</a>, England, with his mother Kezia.<sup id="cite_ref-oliver_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oliver-104"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Ruth_Ndesandjo"></span>Ruth Ndesandjo</dt>
<dd>Born Ruth Beatrice Baker, in US c. 1937, to Maurice Joseph Baker and Ida Baker of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newton,_Massachusetts" title="Newton, Massachusetts">Newton, Massachusetts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Jacobs_2011_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jacobs_2011-105"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup> Ruth was a 1954 graduate of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brookline_High_School" title="Brookline High School">Brookline High School</a> in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brookline,_Massachusetts" title="Brookline, Massachusetts">Brookline, Massachusetts</a>, and a 1958 graduate of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simmons_College_(Massachusetts)" title="Simmons College (Massachusetts)">Simmons College</a> in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a> with a degree in business.<sup id="cite_ref-Jacobs_2011_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jacobs_2011-105"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup> Ruth was a suburban elementary school teacher when she met and began dating Barack Sr. in Cambridge in June 1964, a month before Barack Sr.'s return to Kenya in August 1964.<sup id="cite_ref-Jacobs_2011_105-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jacobs_2011-105"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup> Ruth followed Obama Sr. back to Kenya five weeks later, and married him in Kenya in a civil ceremony on December 24, 1964.<sup id="cite_ref-Jacobs_2011_105-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jacobs_2011-105"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup> She later became a private kindergarten director in Kenya.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106"><span>[</span>107<span>]</span></a></sup> Ruth's two sons with Barack Obama, Sr., are Mark and David Ndesandjo; her third son, Joseph Ndesandjo, was born c. 1980 from a subsequent marriage.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Mark_Ndesandjo"></span>Mark Okoth Obama Ndesandjo</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's half-brother, son of Ruth Nidesand and Barack Obama Sr.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107"><span>[</span>108<span>]</span></a></sup> He runs an Internet company called WorldNexus that advises Chinese corporations how best to reach international customers.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108"><span>[</span>109<span>]</span></a></sup> Mark graduated from <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brown_University" title="Brown University">Brown University</a>, studied <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Physics" title="Physics">physics</a> at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanford_University" title="Stanford University">Stanford University</a>, received an <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Master_of_Business_Administration" title="Master of Business Administration">MBA</a> from <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emory_University" title="Emory University">Emory University</a>, and has lived in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shenzhen,_China" title="Shenzhen, China" class="mw-redirect">Shenzhen, China</a>, since 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109"><span>[</span>110<span>]</span></a></sup> Through his mother, he is Jewish<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110"><span>[</span>111<span>]</span></a></sup> and is married to Liu Xuehua (also spelled Liu Zue Hua in some reports), a <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a> woman from <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henan_Province" title="Henan Province" class="mw-redirect">Henan Province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SZDaily_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SZDaily-111"><span>[</span>112<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112"><span>[</span>113<span>]</span></a></sup> He is also an accomplished pianist.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113"><span>[</span>114<span>]</span></a></sup> In November 2009, he held a press conference for the upcoming publication of his semi-autobiographical novel <i>Nairobi to Shenzhen</i>, and stated that he also planned to write a proper autobiography which would go into more detail about his relationship with Barack Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114"><span>[</span>115<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="David_Ndesandjo"></span>David Ndesandjo (c. 1967 – c. 1987)</dt>
<dd>Barack Obama's half-brother (also known as <b>David Opiyo Obama</b>), son of Ruth Nidesand and Barack Obama Sr. Killed in a motorcycle accident.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115"><span>[</span>116<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116"><span>[</span>117<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="George_Hussein_Onyango_Obama"></span>George Hussein Onyango Obama</dt>
<dd>Youngest half-brother of Barack Obama, born c.1982, son of Barack Obama Sr.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117"><span>[</span>118<span>]</span></a></sup> and Jael Otieno (now a resident of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlanta,_Georgia" title="Atlanta, Georgia" class="mw-redirect">Atlanta, Georgia</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-myinspiration_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-myinspiration-118"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-lifegood_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lifegood-119"><span>[</span>120<span>]</span></a></sup> George was six months old when his father died in an automobile accident, after which he was raised in Nairobi by his mother and a French step-father. He later lived in South Korea for two years while his mother resided there for business reasons.<sup id="cite_ref-myinspiration_118-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-myinspiration-118"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup> Returning to Kenya, George Obama "slept rough for several years,"<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120"><span>[</span>121<span>]</span></a></sup> until his aunt gave him a six-by-eight foot corrugated metal shack in the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>, slum of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huruma_Flats" title="Huruma Flats" class="mw-redirect">Huruma Flats</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-myinspiration_118-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-myinspiration-118"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup> As of August 2008, Obama was studying to become a mechanic.<sup id="cite_ref-myinspiration_118-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-myinspiration-118"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup> George received little attention until being featured in an article in the Italian language edition of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vanity_Fair_(magazine)" title="Vanity Fair (magazine)"><i>Vanity Fair</i></a> in August 2008, which portrayed him as living in poverty, shame, and obscurity.<sup id="cite_ref-cnngo_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnngo-121"><span>[</span>122<span>]</span></a></sup> The article quoted George Obama as saying that he lived "on less than a dollar a month" and stated that he "does not mention his famous half-brother in conversation" out of shame at his poverty.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraph20081020_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraph20081020-122"><span>[</span>123<span>]</span></a></sup> In later interviews George contradicted this picture. In an interview with <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Times" title="The Times">The Times</a></i>, he "said that he was furious at subsequent reports that he had been abandoned by the Obama family and that he was filled with shame about living in a slum."<sup id="cite_ref-lifegood_119-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lifegood-119"><span>[</span>120<span>]</span></a></sup> He told <i>The Times</i>, "Life in Huruma is good." George Obama said that he expects no favors, that he was supported by relatives, and that reports he lived on a dollar a month were "all lies by people who don’t want my brother to win.”<sup id="cite_ref-lifegood_119-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lifegood-119"><span>[</span>120<span>]</span></a></sup> He told <i>The Telegraph</i> that he was inspired by his half-brother.<sup id="cite_ref-myinspiration_118-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-myinspiration-118"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup> According to <i>Time</i>, George "has repeatedly denied...that he feels abandoned by Obama."<sup id="cite_ref-timego_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-timego-123"><span>[</span>124<span>]</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a></i> quoted him as saying, "I was brought up well. I live well even now. The magazines, they have exaggerated everything... I think I kind of like it here. There are some challenges, but maybe it is just like where you come from, there are the same challenges."<sup id="cite_ref-cnngo_121-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnngo-121"><span>[</span>122<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Omar_Okech_Obama"></span>Omar Okech Obama</dt>
<dd>He sometimes goes by a variation of the name of his father <b>Onyango Obama</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe083111_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe083111-124"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BosHerald083111_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosHerald083111-125"><span>[</span>126<span>]</span></a></sup> Half-uncle of Barack Obama,<sup id="cite_ref-familytree_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree-126"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup> born on June 3, 1944 in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyang%E2%80%99oma_Kogelo" title="Nyang’oma Kogelo">Nyang’oma Kogelo</a>. Oldest son of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Onyango_Obama" title="Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Onyango</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Onyango_Obama" title="Sarah Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Sarah Obama</a>, he moved to the U.S. in 1963 as part of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tom_Mboya" title="Tom Mboya">Tom Mboya</a>'s Airlift Africa project.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe083111_124-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe083111-124"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup> Once he arrived in the U.S., Barack Obama Sr. found him a place at a boys’ school then known as Browne &amp; Nichols, in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cambridge,_Massachusetts" title="Cambridge, Massachusetts">Cambridge, Massachusetts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe083111_124-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe083111-124"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup> He later dropped out of school and changed his name to O. Onyango Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe083111_124-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe083111-124"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup> He operated a liquor store in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Framingham,_Massachusetts" title="Framingham, Massachusetts">Framingham, Massachusetts</a>, where he resided as of March 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe083111_124-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe083111-124"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127"><span>[</span>128<span>]</span></a></sup> He was subject to a deportation order in 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe090911_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe090911-128"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boston_Herald" title="Boston Herald">Boston Herald</a> reports that he may have illegally obtained a driver's license and Social Security Number.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129"><span>[</span>130<span>]</span></a></sup> After an unsuccessful appeal he was given a new deportation order in 1992.<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe090911_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe090911-128"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup> He was arrested on August 24, 2011 for <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Driving_under_the_influence" title="Driving under the influence">driving under the influence</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe090911_128-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe090911-128"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup> and subsequently held in jail until September 9, 2011, on a federal immigration warrant.<sup id="cite_ref-BosHerald083111_125-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosHerald083111-125"><span>[</span>126<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BosGlobe091011_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BosGlobe091011-131"><span>[</span>132<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Zeituni_Onyango"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zeituni_Onyango" title="Zeituni Onyango">Zeituni Onyango</a></dt>
<dd>Half-aunt of Barack Obama,<sup id="cite_ref-MSNBC_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MSNBC-132"><span>[</span>133<span>]</span></a></sup> born May 29, 1952, in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-theaustralian_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theaustralian-133"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup> Onyango is referred to as "Aunti Zeituni" in the memoir <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dreams_from_My_Father" title="Dreams from My Father">Dreams from My Father</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134"><span>[</span>135<span>]</span></a></sup> She was denied <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Political_asylum" title="Political asylum" class="mw-redirect">political asylum</a> in the US in 2004, but remained in the country illegally. Her presence was leaked to the media during Barack Obama's 2008 presidential campaign. She was granted asylum in 2010.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Yusuf_Obama"></span>Yusuf Obama</dt>
<dd>Half-uncle of Barack Obama,<sup id="cite_ref-familytree_126-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree-126"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup> born c. 1950s in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyang%E2%80%99oma_Kogelo" title="Nyang’oma Kogelo">Nyang’oma Kogelo</a>; son of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Onyango_Obama" title="Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Onyango</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Onyango_Obama" title="Sarah Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Sarah Obama</a>.<sup class="Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources from November 2008">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Said_Obama"></span>Sayid Obama</dt>
<dd>Half-uncle of Barack Obama,<sup id="cite_ref-familytree_126-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree-126"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135"><span>[</span>136<span>]</span></a></sup> born c. 1950s in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nyang%E2%80%99oma_Kogelo" title="Nyang’oma Kogelo">Nyang’oma Kogelo</a>; son of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Onyango_Obama" title="Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Onyango</a> and <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Onyango_Obama" title="Sarah Onyango Obama" class="mw-redirect">Sarah Obama</a>.<sup class="Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources from November 2008">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></dd>
</dl>
