<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Family_of_Barack_Obama.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Family_of_Barack_Obama.jpg/220px-Family_of_Barack_Obama.jpg" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Family_of_Barack_Obama.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://bits.wikimedia.org/skins-1.19/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt=""/></a></div>
Marian Robinson (second from right) makes an appearance with the rest of the immediate family of Barack Obama on the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blue_Room_(White_House)" title="Blue Room (White House)">South Portico</a> of the White House during festivities of the 2009 <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_House_Easter_Egg_Roll" title="White House Easter Egg Roll" class="mw-redirect">White House Easter Egg Roll</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Barack Obama has called his wife <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michelle_Obama" title="Michelle Obama">Michelle</a> "the most quintessentially American woman I know."<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> Her family is of <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African-American" title="African-American" class="mw-redirect">African-American</a> heritage, descendents of Africans of the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colonial_history_of_the_United_States" title="Colonial history of the United States">American Colonial Era</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> Michelle Obama's family history traces back from <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slavery_in_the_United_States" title="Slavery in the United States">slavery</a> to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reconstruction_era_of_the_United_States" title="Reconstruction era of the United States" class="mw-redirect">Reconstruction</a> to the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Migration_(African_American)" title="Great Migration (African American)">Great Migration North</a>. Some of Michelle's relatives still reside in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">South Carolina</a>.</p>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Jim_Robinson"></span>Jim Robinson</dt>
</dl>
<p>Michelle's earliest known relative on her father's side is her great-great grandfather Jim Robinson, born in the 1850s, who was an American <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slave</a> on the Friendfield plantation in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgetown,_South_Carolina" title="Georgetown, South Carolina">Georgetown, South Carolina</a>. The family believes that after the Civil War he remained a Friendfield plantation <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sharecropper" title="Sharecropper" class="mw-redirect">sharecropper</a> for the rest of his life and that he was buried there in an unmarked grave.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Jim married twice, first to a woman named Louiser with whom had two sons, Gabriel and Fraser, Michelle Obama's great-grandfather. There was also a daughter born to the family, but there is no reference to a name and she is believed to have died as a child. His second marriage to Rose Ella Cohen bore 6 other children. Fraser had an arm amputated as a result of a boyhood injury. He worked as a shoemaker, newspaper salesman and in a lumber mill.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup> Carrie Nelson, Gabriel Robinson's daughter, now 80, is the oldest living Robinson and the keeper of family lore.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>At least three of Michelle Obama's great-uncles served in the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Military_of_the_United_States" title="Military of the United States" class="mw-redirect">military of the United States</a>. One aunt moved to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Princeton,_New_Jersey" title="Princeton, New Jersey">Princeton, New Jersey</a>, where she worked as a maid, and cooked <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soul_food" title="Soul food">Southern-style meals</a> for Michelle and her brother, Craig, when they were students at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Princeton_University" title="Princeton University">Princeton University</a>.</p>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Marian_Lois_Robinson"></span>Marian Lois Robinson</dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's mother (birthname Marian Lois Shields, born July 30, 1937), now widowed, married Michelle's father, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fraser_Robinson" title="Fraser Robinson" class="mw-redirect">Fraser Robinson</a>, on October 27, 1960.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-radaronline.com_137-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-radaronline.com-137"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup> Robinson was formerly a secretary at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spiegel_(catalog)" title="Spiegel (catalog)">Spiegel catalog</a> and a bank. While Michelle and Barack Obama were campaigning in 2008, Robinson tended the Obama's young children and does the same while currently living in the White House itself as part of the First Family;<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup> she is the first live-in grandmother there since <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elivera_M._Doud" title="Elivera M. Doud">Elivera M. Doud</a> during the Eisenhower administration.<sup id="cite_ref-AFPfamilyaffair_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AFPfamilyaffair-139"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup> Some media outlets have dubbed Robinson the "First Granny".<sup id="cite_ref-AFPfamilyaffair_139-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AFPfamilyaffair-139"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup> Marian takes Sasha and Malia to school daily and enjoys life in Washington.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>142<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Fraser_Robinson_III"></span>Fraser C. Robinson III</dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's father, born August 1, 1935, died March 6, 1991, married Michelle's mother, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marian_Shields_Robinson" title="Marian Shields Robinson" class="mw-redirect">Marian Shields</a>, on October 27, 1960.<sup id="cite_ref-radaronline.com_137-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-radaronline.com-137"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142"><span>[</span>143<span>]</span></a></sup> Robinson was a pump worker at the City of Chicago water plant.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
<dt><span id="Craig_Robinson_.28basketball_coach.29"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Craig_Robinson_(basketball_coach)" title="Craig Robinson (basketball coach)" class="mw-redirect">Craig Robinson</a></dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's brother, born 1962. He is currently <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Head_coach" title="Head coach">head coach</a> of men's <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a> at <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oregon_State_University" title="Oregon State University">Oregon State University</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143"><span>[</span>144<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Fraser_Robinson.2C_Jr."></span>Fraser Robinson, Jr.</dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's grandfather was born on August 24, 1912, in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgetown,_South_Carolina" title="Georgetown, South Carolina">Georgetown, South Carolina</a>, and died on November 9, 1996, aged 84. He was a good student and orator, but moved from South Carolina to Chicago to find better work than he could find at home, eventually becoming a worker for the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">United States Postal Service</a>. He was married to LaVaughn Johnson. When he retired, they moved back to South Carolina.<sup id="cite_ref-soil_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soil-3"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="LaVaughn_Dolores_Johnson"></span>LaVaughn Dolores Johnson</dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's grandmother (February 6, 1915-September 17, 2002) and wife of Fraser Robinson Jr. She was born in Chicago, Illinois, to James Preston Johnson (1880-1920?) and Phoebe (1879-1920?) in Chicago.</dd>
</dl>
<dl>
<dt><span id="Capers_Funnye"></span><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capers_Funnye" title="Capers Funnye">Capers C. Funnye Jr.</a></dt>
<dd>Michelle Obama's first cousin once removed: Funnye’s mother, Verdelle Robinson Funnye (born Verdelle Robinson; August 22, 1930 – April 16, 2000) and Michelle Obama’s paternal grandfather, Fraser Robinson Jr., were siblings. One of America's most prominent African American rabbis, known for acting as a bridge between mainstream Jewry and African Americans.<sup id="cite_ref-weiss_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-weiss-144"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>

<p><br/></p>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Distant_relations">Distant relations</span></h2>
<div class="rellink boilerplate seealso">See also: <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_United_States_Presidents_by_genealogical_relationship" title="List of United States Presidents by genealogical relationship" class="mw-redirect">List of United States Presidents by genealogical relationship</a></div>
<p>According to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Genealogy" title="Genealogy">genealogists</a>, Barack Obama's distant cousins include the multitude of descendants of his maternal ancestors from all along the early-American Atlantic seaboard as well as paternal, Kenyan relations belonging to the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luo_(Kenya_and_Tanzania)" title="Luo (Kenya and Tanzania)" class="mw-redirect">Luo tribe</a>, many descending from a 17th century ancestor named Owiny.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145"><span>[</span>146<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146"><span>[</span>147<span>]</span></a></sup> For example, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a>, the 43rd U.S. president, is the eleventh <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cousin" title="Cousin">cousin</a> of Barack Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147"><span>[</span>148<span>]</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> science writer <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicholas_Wade" title="Nicholas Wade">Nicholas Wade</a> argues that with eleven generations leading back to their common progenitor, Samuel Hinckley, the relationship between the 43rd President and the 44th President is "genetically meaningless".<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148"><span>[</span>149<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<dl>
<dt>Selected genealogical relationships</dt>
</dl>
<table align="left" width="50%" border="1" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="3">
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:John_McCain_official_portrait_2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="John McCain official portrait 2009.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/John_McCain_official_portrait_2009.jpg/60px-John_McCain_official_portrait_2009.jpg" width="60" height="76"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>According to William Reitwiesner he is 22nd cousin 2 times removed.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149"><span>[</span>150<span>]</span></a></sup> According to <i>Ancestors of Barack Hussein Obama: 50 Generations</i> by Lorina Boliq, Senator McCain is also Obama's 24th cousin 6 times removed.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Wild_Bill.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Wild Bill.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Wild_Bill.jpg/46px-Wild_Bill.jpg" width="46" height="69"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wild_Bill_Hickok" title="Wild Bill Hickok">Bill Hickok</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>According to Barack Obama's family lore (and confirmed by the New England Historic Genealogical Society), the President and Hickok are sixth cousins, six-times removed.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150"><span>[</span>151<span>]</span></a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Robert_Duvall_by_David_Shankbone.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Robert Duvall by David Shankbone.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Robert_Duvall_by_David_Shankbone.jpg/64px-Robert_Duvall_by_David_Shankbone.jpg" width="64" height="94"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Duvall" title="Robert Duvall">Robert Duvall</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>Goodnight helped inspire Pulitzer Prize-winning author <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Larry_McMurtry" title="Larry McMurtry">Larry McMurtry</a> to create a protagonist for his novel <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lonesome_Dove_series" title="Lonesome Dove series">series</a> <i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lonesome_Dove" title="Lonesome Dove">Lonesome Dove</a>:</i> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Woodrow_Call" title="Woodrow Call" class="mw-redirect">Woodrow Call</a>. In <i>Dove's</i> television <i>novela,</i> Woodrow Call's partner is <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Augustus_%22Gus%22_McCrae" title="Augustus &quot;Gus&quot; McCrae">Gus McCrae</a>, portrayed by Obama's eighth cousin, twice removed, actor Robert Duvall.<sup id="cite_ref-familytree1_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree1-151"><span>[</span>152<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span title=" since May 2011" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot">dead link</a></i>]</span></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:James_Madison.jpg" class="image"><img alt="James Madison.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/James_Madison.jpg/60px-James_Madison.jpg" width="60" height="73"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Madison" title="James Madison">James Madison</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>It is claimed that Obama may also be distantly related to U.S. Presidents <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Madison" title="James Madison">James Madison</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lyndon_Johnson" title="Lyndon Johnson" class="mw-redirect">Lyndon Johnson</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gerald_Ford" title="Gerald Ford">Gerald Ford</a>, and U.S. Vice President <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dick_Cheney" title="Dick Cheney">Dick Cheney</a>, <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Civil_War" title="U.S. Civil War" class="mw-redirect">U.S. Civil War</a> General <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_E._Lee" title="Robert E. Lee">Robert E. Lee</a>, and actor <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brad_Pitt" title="Brad Pitt">Brad Pitt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-newenglandancestors1_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-newenglandancestors1-152"><span>[</span>153<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span title=" since May 2011" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot">dead link</a></i>]</span></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153"><span>[</span>154<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154"><span>[</span>155<span>]</span></a></sup></td>
</tr>
</table>
<table align="right" width="50%" border="1" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="3">
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Elvis_Presley_1970.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Elvis Presley 1970.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Elvis_Presley_1970.jpg/60px-Elvis_Presley_1970.jpg" width="60" height="92"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elvis_Presley" title="Elvis Presley">Elvis Presley</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>Boliq's research additionally indicates that Elvis Presley is Obama's 21st cousin 3 times removed.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><br/>
<a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Goodnite.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Goodnite.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Goodnite.jpg/62px-Goodnite.jpg" width="62" height="65"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Goodnight" title="Charles Goodnight">Charles Goodnight</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>According to <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicago_Sun-Times" title="Chicago Sun-Times">Chicago Sun-Times</a> reporter Scott Fornek, another Obama progenitor, Catherine Goodnight, was the grandniece of George Goodnight, who was in turn great-grandfather of famed cattleman Charles Goodnight.<sup id="cite_ref-familytree1_151-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree1-151"><span>[</span>152<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span title=" since May 2011" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot">dead link</a></i>]</span></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><br/>
<a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Harry-truman.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Harry-truman.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Harry-truman.jpg/56px-Harry-truman.jpg" width="56" height="72"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_S._Truman" title="Harry S. Truman">Harry S. Truman</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>Actor Duvall is distant cousins with United States President Harry Truman, who's likewise a fourth cousin, four times removed, of Obama's.<sup id="cite_ref-familytree1_151-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-familytree1-151"><span>[</span>152<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span title=" since May 2011" style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot">dead link</a></i>]</span></sup></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<center><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Stieglitz,_Georgia_O%27Keeffe,_1918.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Stieglitz, Georgia O'Keeffe, 1918.jpg" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Stieglitz%2C_Georgia_O%27Keeffe%2C_1918.jpg/60px-Stieglitz%2C_Georgia_O%27Keeffe%2C_1918.jpg" width="60" height="74"/></a><br/>
<small><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgia_O%27Keeffe" title="Georgia O'Keeffe">Georgia O'Keeffe</a></small></center>
</td>
<td>Notable women Obama is related to include painter Georgia O’Keeffe.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><br style="clear:both;"/></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Obama_family_tree.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Obama_family_tree.jpg/220px-Obama_family_tree.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Obama_family_tree.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//web.archive.org/web/20120315144017im_/http://bits.wikimedia.org/skins-1.19/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt=""/></a></div>
<i>From left:</i> Senate Majority Leader <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Reid" title="Harry Reid">Harry Reid</a>, the Director of the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_House_Office_of_Faith-Based_and_Neighborhood_Partnerships" title="White House Office of Faith-Based and Neighborhood Partnerships">White House Office of Faith-Based and Neighborhood Partnerships</a> <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joshua_DuBois" title="Joshua DuBois">Joshua DuBois</a>, and President <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_S._Monson" title="Thomas S. Monson">Thomas S. Monson</a>, the head of the LDS Church, look on as Obama observes a detail on his family <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pedigree_chart" title="Pedigree chart">pedigree chart</a> being pointed out to him by Mormon apostle <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dallin_Oaks" title="Dallin Oaks" class="mw-redirect">Dallin Oaks</a>. The denomination has presented such compilations to several recent US presidents.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Five volumes of family genealogy (as compiled at the <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints" title="Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints" class="mw-redirect">Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints</a>' <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Family_History_Library" title="Family History Library">Family History Library</a> in <a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salt_Lake_City,_Utah" title="Salt Lake City, Utah" class="mw-redirect">Salt Lake City, Utah</a>), were presented by Mormon leaders to Obama in July 2009. In a statement, Obama said he was "looking forward to reading through the materials with my daughters. It’s something our family will treasure for years to come."<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156"><span>[</span>157<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/web/20120315144017/http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moneygall" title="Moneygall">Moneygall</a>, Ireland, resident Henry Healy, Barack Obama's eighth cousin, became known for having initiated a visit by the U.S. president in May 2011 to Healy's hometown.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157"><span>[</span>158<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
